The General Fund of the State Budget of Ukraine has received 189.32 million Euro financing from the World Bank.

Funds provided on preferential terms from the International Development Association, reportsMinistry of Finance of Ukraine.

Money will be directed to partial reimbursement of budget expenditures for the payment of employees of state and employees for February 2023.

"The borrowed funds will allow to reimburse the primary social expenditures of the state budget, in particular, the financing of the remuneration of employees of the budgetary sphere, as well as to provide sustainable public administration in Ukraine," said Finance Minister Sergey Marchenko.

How to create a reliable password for accounts - Tips of the State Secret ‚Äô Land

Author: ['–ê–†–ú–Ü–ØINFORM']

Time: 2023-05-09T31:00:00-04:00

Description: The sovereign service of the special Zv'yazka is to Zachist —ñnformasy illegitimate day of password ... War with Ukraine 2022, war with Ukraine Latest news today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, the war with Ukraine In 2022 it will be or not, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukraine‚Äôs news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['screenshot_18-3.jpg']

Tags: ['–í–Ü–ô–ù–ê', '–î–ï–†–ñ–°–ü–ï–¶–ó–í‚Äô–Ø–ó–ö–£']

Category: News

The State Special Communications and Information Protection Service has explained the worldwide password how to create a reliable password for e-mail, social networks and any other accounts.

The State Security Service reportedUtegram.

It is noted that the use of "strong" passwords for bank applications, e-mail boxes, pages on social networks or any other accounts is one of the basic rules of cybergigiene, the observance of which helps to protect data from theft.

The State Secretariat has recalled that a reliable password should contain more than eight symbols: uppercase and lowercase letters, numbers, special characters.

It is effective to use pasphrase. It is a set of words encrypted by the user. For example, a line from a poem, a song in which the spaces are deleted, some literalized in numbers, special symbols, certain letters are translated into upper case.

A strong password can also be created using special passwords.

It is important for each account to have a separate, unique password.

If it is difficult to remember a lot of difficult passwords, you can use passwords - programs that serve as a "safe", allow you to keep your passwords safe with encryption. Passwords can be used on computers and smartphones. When choosing the best advantage of programs of well -known developers, before installing a product reputation, and to study safety reviews.

At the same time, the State Secretariat has warned from the use of simple words in passwords, common combinations of letters and words, symbols that are repeated or go one in the way.

"Combinations such as 123456, Qwerty, Password and the like are categorically bored, hackers break such passwords in less than a second," the service said.

You should not use your own name, last name, date of birth. The same applies to the names, names and any personal information of relatives.

News Source: https://armyinform.com.ua/2023/05/09/yak-stvoryty-nadijnyj-parol-do-oblikovyh-zapysiv-porady-derzhspeczzvyazku/

The Russian Federation refused to register and carry out inspections of ships that will interfere with the "grain corridor" to the entrance to the seaports of Ukraine.

About it reportsThe press service of the Ministry of Community Development, Territories and Infrastructure of Ukraine Ufeysbook.

‚ÄúThe Russian Federation has once again stopped the grain initiative, refusing to register the vessels for entrance and carry out their inspections. Such an approach is contrary to the terms of the current agreement, ‚Äùthe message reads.

The ministry emphasizes that the destructive policy of Russia makes it impossible to draw up an inspection plan in accordance with the procedures of a joint coordination center, which provides for daily approval by all parties of the plan of inspections of both exit and entry.

As of May 8, 2023, 90 vessels are being inspected in the territorial waters of Turkey, of which 62 are ships that go under loading. Inspection as an entrance and output fleet are suspended.

‚ÄúUkraine categorically does not accept Russia's efforts to stop the registration of the and inspection of the entrance fleet, which should be held in view of working on working. We expect partners, the UN and Turkey, ‚Äùthe UNSC is emphasized.

Type: Article

Initially, the invasion of Ukraine did not create a system of logistics, suffered heavy losses, and now forced to use obsolete equipment and untrained people in large number.

This was announced today in Brussels during a press conference following the meeting of the Defense of the Defense of the Union countries, the head of the Military Committee, Nathoadmiral Rob Bauer, Ukrinform correspondent reports.

At the same time, Ukraine, according to him, focuses on the quality of forces and drunking of servicemen, uses weapons of Western samples, and this cut will be reflected on the battlefield over the following months.

‚ÄúAny side in the war faces the same problems-loses people, has destroyed or damaged equipment, and feels a lack of ammunition. One of the aid miscalculations that Russia admitted - they were preparing for a three -day, "forgot" to inform performers about its goals and could not deploy a logistics system. So during the days they were left without fuel for the tank armies, ‚Äùsaid NATO military director.

Read also:

He noted that in the context of hostilities on the fourth or sixth day, they are transformed into logistics competitions, and this is what happens in Ukraine currently. This is closely related to other problems-with the ability to replenish stools, receive new equipment, tanks and combat vehicles, tanks and combat vehicles, tanks and combat vehicles new artillery systems and more. It is also about replenishing the personnel of the conscription or mobilization and its preparation.

‚ÄúFrom a material point of view, the Russians began to use very old-materials and capabilities, for example, the T-54 tanks, the 1954 model, which we mibble on the battlefield. The problem is that they still have a lot of these-54. We see that the Russians are forced to focus on quantities. Including a large number of conscripts and mobilized people who are not well -known, they act on outdated materials, but in large numbers. Ukrainian, on the other hand, focused on quality, with weapons of the Western design, and as appropriate training for the military. This is a big difference that will have the manifestation of the next months, ‚ÄùNATO Military Committee said.He confirmed that after the beginning of Russian aggression in Ukraine with certain logistics problems, allies on the Alliance were also faced, as they were not ready for such a large -scale war of high intensity.

‚ÄúLogistics and logistics environment is a very important component(prompt - ed.)thinking. For many decades, we have neglected a large volume that would be related to collective defense to a large -scale conflict - because we did not provide such a conflict. We planned smaller operations, which also had a significant logistics component, but were much more suitable for planning than war we see in Ukraine now, ‚ÄùBauer said.

Read also:

He stressed that the solution of such problems is not a matter of one day, it will interfere with large -scale and long efforts and investments, including in the development of the system of providing troops and logistics, improving the system of military management, etc. All this is at the heart of updated operational concepts on the modernization of the structure of troops and their provision, which will be considered during NATO -Samite in Vilnius.

In turn, the Commander -in -Chief of the United NATO Armed Forces in Europian -American General Christopher Cavola(Christopher Cavoli)He noted that it is not necessary to underestimate the Russian army.

‚ÄúI want to add that the degradation of the Russian Armed Forces is really unprecedented. Alevona concerns, above all, land forces, why we have very multifaceted. In Ukraine, there will be a maximum of Europe in Europe - the maximum of the possible European values, which is capable of European and global cooperation.

President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky, Ukrinform reports about it in his address at the end of the 441th day of a full-scale war.

Video: _ I wish health, dear Ukrainians!_

Briefly about today, about our actions.

Our international block is very active, in detail works with partners for the sake of new -shaped packages for Ukraine. New solutions are already at the working level. More deficiency for our sky, more opportunities for our defense and the Movement. I held several meetings today, where we discussed it all. And we expect the corresponding steps from partners to the next time.

Neither for a moment we do not forget that every day the presence of the occupier on our earth is a temptation to think for him as if he would succeed. He will not see nothing!We need to return freedom, security and Europe to all Ukrainian land - all European land. We will do it!Let's not leave the enemy of any shredded land - no tyranny will rule. And I thank the partner leaders, all the partner states, everyone and everyone who helps us to strengthen our power and make Ukrainian defense even more active.

He held a rather meaningful meeting with government officials on the renewal of the territory and Ukrainian life after hostilities and war in general. We are working out all the aspects of recovery, and each of them is in a new security form. Economics and industry, defense, energy, energy, infrastructure, educational industry, social sphere, medicine, in particular the rehabilitation component ... All that should be built, what is ready to invest in the world, what will give Ukraine and Ukrainians reliable protection and confident development .

Now, during May, we will refine the specific points of these state programs, and in June we will go for practical work with partners on our plans. The reconstruction here and now - critical systems and strategic transformation of our country. I am sure that our project will give impetus for development at least all our region - after Ukraine, and to all our partners who will cooperate with Ukraine.Step by step, on the basis of the resources that we now implement the proficiency recovery of our country. In particular, the state service "Equation" was employed today. It is the support of people who need to repair the houses of the apquards after damaging war. Already this day we have a considerable amount of application "Action". In general, it is about hundreds of thousands of damaged objects. Moreover, we also have to work out this task as to those of our people who were able to force the damaged home. Equality in help is very important, the algorithm is needed. The next step is to compensate for the lost life. And it will be.

Of course, during the day I communicated with our commander, with intelligence executives. The situation on the forefront is the obvious first priority.

Today he has signed new decrees on the celebration of our warriors by state -owned. The 10th Separate Mountain Assault Brigade. 14th, 28, 53, 59-Tai 72 Separate mechanized brigades. 3rd Separate Storm Brigade. 27-Mareactive Artillery Brigade. 112th separate team TRO. 67th Separate Battalion. 65th Military Mobile Hospital. It is a Liman Wash, Bakhmut, Yar, Avdiivskyi, Shakhtarsky.

In total, today the decrees marked 266 of our defenders and defenders. The most echoed, the most worthy are those whose lives are the life of Ukraine, our wonderful art of indomitable Ukraine.

Glory to all our soldiers, who are now in battle, in combat posts and in combat operations!

Glory to every Ukrainian family who raised such sons and daughters!

Glory to Ukraine!

Type: Article

Hungarian studied the next European skating championship, associated with the consequences of war in Ukraine.

This is reported in The Hungarian National Association of Slime Sports, Ukrinform reports.

The European Championships 2024 from figure skating was to take place in Budapest from 22 to 28th.

The Hungarian National Association of Snake Sports reported that they did not have the necessary funds for receiving the tournament Public sport.

The reason for the Hungarian organization was explained by the consequences of the war in Ukraine. It is concerned that due to a full -scale invasion, the prices of napnergonosia increased, which was the main cause of financial difficulties.

‚ÄúDue to the long war in our neighboring country, which has influenced the economy and the energy of energy, which are essential for figure skating, the Hungarian Association refuses to Euro-2024 after long thought. We are reflected in the right to organize an event through a shortage of necessary financial resources for such a high level of competitions, ‚Äùthe organization states.

As a result of the decision to refuse to carry out the tournament, the International Snakers resumed the period of application for its organization. It will last up to 26th.

"It also indicates that together we are much stronger than alone," the Admiral said.

European Commission through the U-LEAD program organizes in Ukraine test pilot projects for school recovery

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: –£–∫—Ä–∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-10T16:09:47+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-10T16:09:47+03:00

Description: The European Commission, through the U-LEAD with Europe program, organizes in Ukraine, test pilot projections for the restoration of schools, for example, which intends to find out how to ensure the return of children in the shortest possible time to education and what ideas are best implemented. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16837...", "1683724027-60..."]

Tags: ['–Ñ–≤—Ä–æ–∫–æ–º—ñ—Å—ñ—è', '–®–∫–æ–ª–∞', 'U-LEAD –∑ –Ñ–≤—Ä–æ–ø–æ—é', '–í—ñ–¥–±—É–¥–æ–≤–∞']

Type: Article

The European Commission, through the U-LEAD with Europe program, organizes in Ukraine the test pilot projects for the restoration of schools, for example, which should intend to ensure the return of children in the shortest possible time to education.

This was stated by the director of the European Commission Foreign Tools Service Wagner during the seminar "Recovery of access to education: dialogue on the role of Ukrainian communities in repair, restoration and reconstruction" in Chernihiv, Ukrinform correspondent reports.

The European Commission Representative noted that, in his opinion, at this stage of renewal of access to education, the maximum cooperation with the state is "absolutely necessary", because the resolution of major strategic issues can begin only the national level.

"But now we are trying to organize pilot test projects, in particular here, because we think it is important not to miss the moment when we will need to move to decentralized implementation," Wagner said.

He added that it is not only about the crisis response, but of all the elements of the European Commission in Ukraine, in particular in the field of decentralization, which was one of the most successful reform projects in the period after Euromaidan.

‚ÄúWe combine decentralization with this great need to restore education and a magnificent number of needs that have now arisen. In our opinion, now for this potential, so we say: let's use the existing U -LEAD structure, because there are already partners who work throughout the country, ‚Äùsaid the director of the ECE.

According to him, European partners are now seeking to understand whether they will be able to quickly and successfully implement such projects that will allow children to return to , as well as to find out which ideas are really better to implement.

In this context, he noted that there are elements that are much better implemented at the local or regional level, which "the state does not understand."

According to Wagner, he looks forward to the moment when the schools begin to see at what level you can organize different parts of these pilot projects.He noted that European partners are generally interested in how much you need online.

Read also: Ukraine partnership UNDON UNOPS * Recover * 100 schools regions ‚ÄúNow we have realized that it was needed, that online learning is doing an important role. I also look forward to the view of military administrations that will differentiate from how we have imagined it to war or imagine the postwar. There is an obligation, there is an understanding, but we also need to understand what is the most needed and the most targeted ways of support ‚Äù, - summarized the Director of the European Commission of Foreign Policy.

The program for Ukraine for the expansion of rights and opportunities at the local level, accountability and development of "U-LEAD with Europe" is jointly funded by the EU and its states-members of Germany, Poland, Sweden, Denmia, Estonia and Slovenia to support Ukraine on its way to strengthen local self-government. U-LEAD promotes transparent, accountable and multilevel administration in Ukraine, which responds to citizens' needs and expands communities.

The Deputy Minister of Agrarian Policy and Food of Ukraine from Digital Development, Digital Transformations and Digitalization Denisbashlyk during the press conference at the Media Center Ukraine - Ukrinform.

"In fact, for 4 months of 2023 we have 13,000 sales agreements(narinku - Aut.). –ü—Ä–∏ —Ü—å–æ–º—É —Ü—ñ–Ω–∞ –≤—Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–Ω—å–æ–º—É –∑—Ä–æ—Å–ª–∞ –Ω–∞ 20%", - —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–≤ –≤—ñ–Ω.

Developed by the Ministry of Agrarian Policy, in the Lviv region as of the beginning of May, the average hectare of one hectare of agricultural land is 162 thousand UAH, while at the time of market opening it amounted to UAH 51 thousand.

In the Kyiv region, one hectare of land costs 148 thousand UAH, while at the beginning of the functioning of the market it cost 48 thousand UAH.

"Even if you buy inflation factor. We see, even in conditional units of growth(prices - ed.)continues. But there is no such growth in regions that are around the fighting, "Bashlyk said.

Since the launch of electronic land auctions in October 2021, the auctions for the purchase and lease of land for more than UAH 1.2 billion have already been completed.

"Since the launch of the first electronic auctions in 2021, the agreement for more than UAH 1.2 billion is being used today. That is the income that sellers and landlords of land plots were held during this time," Seoprozorro said.He added that the total initial cost of sales and renting land plots exposed to electronic auctions was less than UAH 500 million.

Booth noted that on average, three participants come to one auction, which is a display of the popularity of land trading in the system.

As reported by Ukrinform, the land market in Ukraine officially started on July 1, 2021. By 2024, only natural persons-citizens of Ukraine can buy agricultural land with a limitation of 100 hectares. The law on the land market forbids land to foreigners.

Three public organizations -partners of the U -LEAD with Europe -presented their vision of rapid renewal of access to education for children deer or victims of Russian aggression of the territories.

Ukraine this year has exported to the EU about one million tons of soybean

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: –£–∫—Ä–∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-10T17:34:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-10T17:34:00+03:00

Description: Since the beginning of 2023, Ukraine has exported about 1 million tonnes of soybean to the European Union. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_14920..."]

Tags: ['–ï–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç', '–Ñ–≤—Ä–æ—Å–æ—é–∑', '–ê–≥—Ä–∞—Ä—ñ—ó', '–°–æ—è']

Type: Article

In 2023, Ukraine exported about 1 million TSU to the European Union.

The First Deputy Minister of Agrarian Policy and Food of Ukraine Taras Vysotsky told this during the first international non-GMO Summit "Strengthening Market Protection without GMOs"(International Non-GMO Summit), reports Ukrinform with a referral to .

‚ÄúAgrarians continue to sow soybean - a vital culture for the supply of Bilk . In 2022, more than 1.5 million hectares were harvested in Ukraine and 3.7 million tonnes of soybean were harvested, which is 7% more than 2021. Since the beginning of 2023, about 1 million Tutorial soybeans have already been exported to the EU, ‚Äùhe said.

Vysotsky noted that Ukraine, as a candidate for entry into the EU, has been following the EU legislation. In particular, she joined the rules for counter -drilling forests. And since the end of 2024, some agricultural products, such as soybeans, will only be grown in lands where forests have not been cut down.

According to the Deputy Minister, last year about 658 thousand tons of soybean in Ukraine(17.5%of total production)was certified as a stable non-gmo soybean, according to the standards of the Danube Soybean Association. This guarantees the strictness of soybeans of EU norms to protect plants and reduce the emissions of parking gases.

"Such a significant result was achieved in connection with the implementation of the Program of the Protection Partnership, which is aimed at stimulating the sustainable production of non -gmo soybeans," Vysotsky emphasized.

He also said that the Ukrainian government has drafted a bill to strengthen the control, trade, import and export of GMO products, in accordance with EU law. The document provides for a strict punishment for violations of the law in the field of GMO management.

Read also: peas The first international non-GMO Summit is conducted and coordinated by key business associations in the non-GMO market, including the Danube Soybean Association. Samitobunted about 200 participants from 19 countries in South America and Europe to exchange information about the availability and production needs of non-gomo crops.

Type: Article

The Ohmatdit NSSL plans to create the first specialized center for rehabilitation in hospital conditions affected by the Russian armed aggression.

This was reported at the press conference by the medical director of the medical institution Serhiy Chernyshuk, Ukrinform correspondent reports.

"The project is ambitious, it includes serious renovation of the premises that we are currently fired, but are not suitable for providing the proper level of such assistance. It will also include the purchase We will not only improve the conditions, but also expand the spectrum of rehabilitation assistance that we can provide our patients, "Chernyshuk said.

He noted that rehabilitation is a compulsory component of medical care and is due to the moment when the patient is still in intensive care.

According to him, it is planned that the department will have 14 beds for the need for rehabilitation assistance, which will allow to unload other departments, where children after specialized treatment have become rehabilitated, as well as to rehabilitate patients who do not live in Kiev. This also applies to cases where rehabilitation is long, for example, in the case of prosthetics after limb amputation.

Read also: "Fortunately, children with amputations are not much during the war as adults, there are also experiences. We already have experience and prosthetics and preparations for prosthetics, and adaptation for prosthesis. It will be one of the directions, these children need long -lasting. It is important about the months, and at this time it is important for the child to deover, "Chernyshuk said.

In addition, in Many patients with disadvantage, orthopedic problems that can also need to need to need to be needed after the main treatment for a long time.

The medical director noted that in Okhmatdita training of medical students on physical rehabilitologists, ergotherapists, they already work as the help of doctors and in the future will be able to work at the rehabilitation center.The project is implemented(Lok), which began to raise funds for the creation of a stationary department of rehabilitation.

According to Cyril Novikov Charitable Foundation Charitable Foundation, it is planned to repair the premises of the old surgical building with an area of 600 square meters, where all networks will be completely replaced, internal arrangement.

"The approximate cost of this stage is about UAH 15 million. The second part of the estimate is the medical equipment, the equipment of the wards, the rehabilitation, medical equipment. The total estimated cost of the project today is UAH 40 million," - said Nonovikov.

According to Novikov, the fund from the beginning of a full -scale invasion of cooperation with exaggerated donors, some of the funds can be raised on the fundraising platform.

In particular, the department plans a premises for prosthetics/orthotics, rooms for ergotherapy, physical therapy halls, and the conditions for work with burn injury, with pediatric surgery are being created.

Read also: It is also planned to create two separate chambers for sensory deprivation for patients after severe injuries or surgery that require complete resting conditions for recovery.

In general, it is planned to buy more than 190 units of medical rehabilitation equipment, including electroneuromiograph, rehabilitation treadmill, suspension system with adaptive unloading regulation, verticals, patient monitors, medical beds, rehabilitation complex of topics.

During the year, the department will be able to accept up to 290 children from all regions of Ukraine, the total number of patients who will be able to receive rehabilitation services will be up to 3000 people.

More than 11,000 local government representatives from 55 countries have united to stimulate the development of green energy and reduce the number of harmful emissions. Read also: garden The Agreement of Mayors is the world's largest climate conservation movement and the local level. This European initiative brings together thousands of local authorities who have voluntarily undertaken to achieve the EU's climatic and energy goals. The signatories undertake to take measures to achieve the reduction of greenhouse gas emissions by at least 35% by 2030 and adaptation to the effects of climate change.

He was one of the first Ukrainian cities, which in 2009 joined the Agreement of Mayors and successfully fulfilled its obligations - by 2020 it reduced the emission of CO2 by 20.3%.

According to the data of the Ukrainian Food Safety and Consumer Protection Service, 45 operators of the Ukrainian market have the right to export dairy products.

According to Ukrinform, with reference to a statement by the so -called. Olga Shevchenko's Holovyid Consumer Service reports It is noted that 19 Ukrainian manufacturers were granted the right to export dairy products in 2022. In 2023, 5 manufacturers were granted this right.

"That is, in fact, half of the exporters appeared during the martial law," Shevchenko said.

Such demand on the part of Ukrainian producers of dairy products is caused by the possibility of European logistics. The head of the State Consumer Service has announced that more and more domestic producers meet the demanding and European legislation.

Read also: "And given that the export of dairy products has become possible since 2016, the period 2022-2023 demonstrates excellent rates of increasing the number of exporters," she said.

Shevchenko also reported that negotiations with Canada, India and Oktya are ongoing. According to her, the State Consumer Service awaits information from representatives of Ukrainian dairy business to the countries in which they are interested in exporting their products.

As reported by Ukrinform, in 2022 31 Ukrainian producer of food products received the right to to the EU.

‚ÄúIn general, police in the territories 385 bodies were found, 309 of them were cynoviored. DNA shows are selected to identify the body and comparative examinations with possible relatives are conducted.

Kyivstar has allocated 10 million for the children's burn department of the Unbreakable Center in Lviv

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Description: Kyivstar has allocated 10 million hryvnias for the purchase of medical equipment for the children's burn department of the Unbreakable Center in Lviv. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16837...", "630_360_16837...", "630_360_16837...", "630_360_16837...", "630_360_16837...", "630_360_16837...", "630_360_16837..."]

Tags: ['–î—ñ—Ç–∏', '–õ—å–≤—ñ–≤', '–ë–ª–∞–≥–æ–¥—ñ–π–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å', '–ö–∏—ó–≤—Å—Ç–∞—Ä', '–¶–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä ¬´–ù–µ–∑–ª–∞–º–Ω—ñ¬ª']

Type: Article

Kyivstarvidyd 10 million hryvnias for the purchase of medical equipment for children's care for the Unbreakable Center in Lviv.

This was reported during a briefing at the National Rehabilitation Center "Unbreakable", Ukrinform correspondent reports.

The company is united with DOBRO.UA and the Center "Unbreakable" and expands the healthy program "Children's Hope" in a new direction - helping children with burns.

‚ÄúWe want to be not only a technological company, but also that helps people to understand the consequences of this war. We focused on key issues - support of military, hospitals, victims of war and reconstruction of Ukraine. Currently, the problem of burns is important in our country, the victims of explosions are often victims, and we have allocated 10 million hryvnias to buy critical equipment, ‚Äùsaid Konstar Konstantin Evening.

He also stressed that all Kyivstar subscribers may join a well-made action for the help of the Children's Burning Branch of the National Rehabilitation Center "Unbreakable", for this purpose it is possible to transfer funds of up to three thousand hryvnias by SMS-notification to the room 45 00 25 **. IVSi funds will be transferred to the purchase of a laser for the treatment of scars after burns.

Read also: Kyivstar According to the CEO of the First Medical Association of Lviv Oleg Samchuk, the National Rehabilitation Center "Unbreakable" from the first days of full -scale interaction became one of the main shelves for which were affected by the war. Over the last year, the number of hospitalizations has increased 5 times-from 20 a day to 100 a day. The doctor has accepted more than 3,000 children from all over Ukraine who were running away, 250 of them with mine-explosive lesions and burns. Central doctors are giving highly specialized medical care and rehabilitation. However, because of the necessary conditions and medical equipment of the most severe children with burns of Ukraine, it is forced to send abroad.‚ÄúThe war made adjustments to medicine. We actually create the children's burn ward from scratch, because before the full -scale invasion of adult patients did not divide, and there is a considerable difference in the protocols of treatment of tarerabilitation. We are studying the experience of experts from around the world, but for full work we need to improve the conditions and buy expensive equipment. After all, patients with burn require extremely demanding conditions of Isanitary standards. We now redirect children with severe burns in the United States, but also can be treated with us, because we have cool specialists, however, it is necessary to create favorable conditions for this, ‚ÄùSamchuk added.

Read also: As reported by Ukrinform, the National Rehabilitation Center "Unbreakable"(‚ÄúUnbroken‚Äù)- It is a place where adults and children who have suffered from the war receive a comprehensive qualified medical care. These are reconstructive regurgy, orthopedics and working prosthetics. The victims not only determine prostheses, they are made here. In addition, the center is engaged in the physical, psychological and psychosocial rehabilitation of victims of the military and civilians. The project is implemented by the first medical association and Lviv City Council with the support of the Ministry of Health of Ukraine.

In Ukraine, there will be a maximum of Europe in Europe - the maximum of the possible European values, which is capable of European and global cooperation.

President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky, Ukrinform reports about it in his address at the end of the 441th day of a full-scale war.

Briefly about today, about our actions.

Our international block is very active, in detail works with partners for the sake of new -shaped packages for Ukraine. New solutions are already at the working level. More deficiency for our sky, more opportunities for our defense and the Movement. I held several meetings today, where we discussed it all. And we expect the corresponding steps from partners to the next time.

He will not see nothing!We need to return freedom, security and Europe to all Ukrainian land - all European land. We will do it!Let's not leave the enemy of any shredded land - no tyranny will rule. And I thank the partner leaders, all the partner states, everyone and everyone who helps us to strengthen our power and make Ukrainian defense even more active.

He held a rather meaningful meeting with government officials on the renewal of the territory and Ukrainian life after hostilities and war in general. We are working out all the aspects of recovery, and each of them is in a new security form. Economics and industry, defense, energy, energy, infrastructure, educational industry, social sphere, medicine, in particular the rehabilitation component ... All that should be built, what is ready to invest in the world, what will give Ukraine and Ukrainians reliable protection and confident development .

Now, during May, we will refine the specific points of these state programs, and in June we will go for practical work with partners on our plans. The reconstruction here and now - critical systems and strategic transformation of our country. I am sure that our project will give impetus for development at least all our region - after Ukraine, and to all our partners who will cooperate with Ukraine.Step by step, on the basis of the resources that we now implement the proficiency recovery of our country. In particular, the state service "Equation" was employed today. It is the support of people who need to repair the houses of the apquards after damaging war. Already this day we have a considerable amount of application "Action". In general, it is about hundreds of thousands of damaged objects. Moreover, we also have to work out this task as to those of our people who were able to force the damaged home. Equality in help is very important, the algorithm is needed. The next step is to compensate for the lost life. And it will be.

Of course, during the day I communicated with our commander, with intelligence executives. The situation on the forefront is the obvious first priority.

Today he has signed new decrees on the celebration of our warriors by state -owned. The 10th Separate Mountain Assault Brigade. 14th, 28, 53, 59-Tai 72 Separate mechanized brigades. 3rd Separate Storm Brigade. 27-Mareactive Artillery Brigade. 112th separate team TRO. 67th Separate Battalion. 65th Military Mobile Hospital. It is a Liman Wash, Bakhmut, Yar, Avdiivskyi, Shakhtarsky.

In total, today the decrees marked 266 of our defenders and defenders. The most echoed, the most worthy are those whose lives are the life of Ukraine, our wonderful art of indomitable Ukraine.

Glory to all our soldiers, who are now in battle, in combat posts and in combat operations!

Glory to every Ukrainian family who raised such sons and daughters!

Glory to Ukraine!

The war in Ukraine will increasingly contrast the amount of quality - Admiral Bauer

Description: From the beginning of the invasion of Ukraine, Russian invaders have not created a logistics system, have suffered heavy losses, and are now forced to use outdated equipment and untrained people in large numbers. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16634..."]

Tags: ['–ù–ê–¢–û', '–£–∫—Ä–∞—ó–Ω–∞', '–ê–≥—Ä–µ—Å—ñ—è –†–§', '–í—ñ–π–Ω–∞ –∑ —Ä–æ—Å—ñ—î—é']

Type: Article

Initially, the invasion of Ukraine did not create a system of logistics, suffered heavy losses, and now forced to use obsolete equipment and untrained people in large number.

This was announced today in Brussels during a press conference following the meeting of the Defense of the Defense of the Union countries, the head of the Military Committee, Nathoadmiral Rob Bauer, Ukrinform correspondent reports.

At the same time, Ukraine, according to him, focuses on the quality of forces and drunking of servicemen, uses weapons of Western samples, and this cut will be reflected on the battlefield over the following months.

‚ÄúAny side in the war faces the same problems-loses people, has destroyed or damaged equipment, and feels a lack of ammunition. One of the aid miscalculations that Russia admitted - they were preparing for a three -day, "forgot" to inform performers about its goals and could not deploy a logistics system. So during the days they were left without fuel for the tank armies, ‚Äùsaid NATO military director.

Read also:

He noted that in the context of hostilities on the fourth or sixth day, they are transformed into logistics competitions, and this is what happens in Ukraine currently. This is closely related to other problems-with the ability to replenish stools, receive new equipment, tanks and combat vehicles, tanks and combat vehicles, tanks and combat vehicles new artillery systems and more. It is also about replenishing the personnel of the conscription or mobilization and its preparation.

‚ÄúFrom a material point of view, the Russians began to use very old-materials and capabilities, for example, the T-54 tanks, the 1954 model, which we mibble on the battlefield. The problem is that they still have a lot of these-54. We see that the Russians are forced to focus on quantities. Including a large number of conscripts and mobilized people who are not well -known, they act on outdated materials, but in large numbers. Ukrainian, on the other hand, focused on quality, with weapons of the Western design, and as appropriate training for the military. This is a big difference that will have the manifestation of the next months, ‚ÄùNATO Military Committee said.He confirmed that after the beginning of Russian aggression in Ukraine with certain logistics problems, allies on the Alliance were also faced, as they were not ready for such a large -scale war of high intensity.

‚ÄúLogistics and logistics environment is a very important component(prompt - ed.)thinking. For many decades, we have neglected a large volume that would be related to collective defense to a large -scale conflict - because we did not provide such a conflict. We planned smaller operations, which also had a significant logistics component, but were much more suitable for planning than war we see in Ukraine now, ‚ÄùBauer said.

Read also:

He stressed that the solution of such problems is not a matter of one day, it will interfere with large -scale and long efforts and investments, including in the development of the system of providing troops and logistics, improving the system of military management, etc. All this is at the heart of updated operational concepts on the modernization of the structure of troops and their provision, which will be considered during NATO -Samite in Vilnius.

In turn, the Commander -in -Chief of the United NATO Armed Forces in Europian -American General Christopher Cavola(Christopher Cavoli)He noted that it is not necessary to underestimate the Russian army.

‚ÄúI want to add that the degradation of the Russian Armed Forces is really unprecedented. Alevona concerns, above all, land forces, why we have very multifaceted. At the same time, it is worth remembering that in other areas, this degradation is much less noticeable, ‚Äùthe US military commander said.

Read also:

It has already been reported that the NATO Military Committee is the highest body of the Alliance, which determines the needs of defense and development of the Armed Forces to ensure the collective defense of the Allies, to enforce NATO political decisions.

About it reports With reference to knowledgeable sources, Ukrinform reports.

‚ÄúThe official $ 600 million payment was postponed to the next year. The increase in energy prices has been a stronger, "the agency reports with a reference to a knowledgeable source.

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', '–ê–ì–†–ï–°–Ü–Ø –†–§', '–í–ò–ü–õ–ê–¢–ò –î–õ–Ø –í–ü–û', '–í–Ü–ô–ù–ê', '–í–ü–û', '–í–¢–û–†–ì–ù–ï–ù–ù–Ø –†–§', '–ú–Ü–ù–†–ï–Ü–ù–¢–ï–ì–†–ê–¶–Ü–á']

Category: News

Illustrative photo

About it reportsMinistry of Reintegration.

The Pension Fund will automatically assign housing subsidies for non -heating periodoids for most households that received a subsidy in the previous fuel season. This is possible provided that the property of the property or family composition has not changed.

Housing subsidies will also be automatically re -assigned to intraveracted persons who receive them at the registration address.

If an internally displaced person plans to issue a subsidy at a address other than the place of registration, he or she must contact the Pension Fund of Ukraine and submit the relevant application and declaration of income.

Housing subsidies will be assigned on the basis of the services received from the providers on the provision of citizens with housing and communal services invented prices, tariffs and the amount of contributions/payments for the management of the household house and utilities.

In the absence of the necessary information, the housing subsidy for such services will not be determined.

Displaced persons can request a housing subsidy.(https://portal.pfu.gov.ua/sidebar/Templates/InfoSubsidy)Or by giving up to the Fund's service center at the place of actual stay.

A pre -trial investigation into a former law enforcement officer who helped the occupiers in Kupyansk Kharkiv region has been completed. Thus, after the beginning of the Russian invasion of Ukraine, the person voluntarily agreed to work for the Nazagarbniki in the so -called convoy detachment, which was to function on the basis of the Kupyansk occupation militia. At the instructions of the Russian man, he protected illegally detained Ukrainian citizens, participants of the ATO. There are known cases when he beat and mocked the detainees.

After escaping the invaders from Kupyansk, the man stayed in the city and tried to hide. However, he was detained.

The former law enforcement officer is charged with a state treason committed in the conditions of a state.

The sanction of the article provides for a sentence in the form of life imprisonment.

The Ministry of Justice of Ukraine has been transferred to the second mobile DNA laboratory intended for the detection and identification of victims of war in the de-occupied territories. The gift certificate and keys were received by Justice Minister Denis Masus.

As reportsThe Office of the Prosecutor General of Ukraine, the transfer of the laboratory took place on the initiative of the Prosecutor General of Ukraine, theandri Kostin, together with the extraordinary and authorized ambassador of the French Republic to Ukraine Etienne de Ponsen.

The first such laboratory was transferred in August 2022. It has been successfully used by experts in the Kharkiv region.

The DNA laboratory will operate in Dnipropetrovsk and neighboring regions, which will be administered from massive artillery and aviation shelling. These regions were significant destruction and, unfortunately, numerous casualties.

  • So far, law enforcement officials, during the inspection of places, show the bodies of dead citizens, and sometimes places of mass burials. The mobile laboratory will significantly accelerate the process of identifying the dead. Ukrainian experts will be able to take all necessary actions directly at the scene, thereby reducing the time of uncertainty and expectations for relatives and close victims of aggression, - the Prosecutor General of Ukraine stated.

Mr. Etien de Possen noted that since the first days of a large -scale invasion, Frank has supported Ukraine. French experts were the first among foreign partners a year ago to arrive in the de -mentioned cities of Kyiv region to help Ukrainian law enforcement.

The passage of the Military Medical Commission will become faster and more convenient.

About this it is referredin the statement of the Ministry of Defense of Ukraine.

In particular, improving the process of passing the Military Medical Commission provides:

  • increasing the network of VLK due to their additional deployment in civilian health care institutions; * separate financing for the payment of health workers' services, which are involved in conducting medical examinations in order to assess the degree of suitability for military service; * introduction of E-Jergi recording on the VLK, electronic document flow between military units, shopping center and health care facilities; * Involvement of health care facilities from the Ministry of Defense system to work with ESOs. Healthcare facilities from the Defense Ministry will have access to a human history, in particular in an electronic medical card; * Introduction of modern approaches to service during the passage of VLK(Available and convenient service); * Information Support(hotline)and the introduction of information products to help servicemen get help.

The Defense Ministry emphasized that the changes will be gradual, because the process is involved in a number of normative legal acts, technical development of resources.

Category: News

The Government has made a decision that enhances the transparency and publicity of procurement for defense for the Armed Forces of Ukraine, will promote competition and reduce the nutrition services for the country's budget.

About it informsGovernment portal.

The decision approved the procedure for determining the subject of procurement during the implementation of foodstuffs, services for providing food sets, food and food services for the personnel of the Armed Forces of Ukraine.

The key provision of the order is that food is purchased, as exclusively in cases where the cost of related services(In particular, food organization, refreshing)exceeds the cost of the products themselves. The state administration can also identify the type of procurement as services, in the case of food supply in educational establishments and in some military units, the UK does not provide for the presence of chefs or their involvement is impossible from objective reasons.

_ ‚ÄúWe give up the system of purchasing the services that have compromised itself, and we go to the purchase of goods. The purchase of services will remain in minor and will be carried out mainly for military universities, lyceums - degraders for cooking are really provided.

In addition, the decision is unlocked with the possibility of purchase with the use of arranged purchases in the ProZorro system and a list of information for submission by the newspaper prior to the procurement announcement.

The Government also provides the terms of publishing information on the customer's procurement of its list in accordance with the law on the introduction of transparency of wobbed procurement, so that state customers do not have to report twice.With regard to future procurement agreements concluded without the use of electronic procurement system, provided that the cost of the purchased goods of personnel services is equal to or exceeds UAH 200 thousand and works - UAH 1.5 million , the state service must publish information about them During 10 working days after the conclusion. The relevant contracts under such reports must be publicized within 90 days after the end of martial law.

Decisions do not apply to the purchase of goods, works and services of defense, which make up state secret, as well as the purchase of weapons, military special equipment, ammunition and their components and services of development, repair, modernization of weapons, military and special equipment, ammunition and their components.

President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky created two new military administrations of Uherson region.

According to Ukrinform with reference to the President's office, appropriate It was made public on 10th.

"The General Staff of the Armed Forces of Ukraine, the Kherson Regional State Administration should be carried out in accordance with the Law of Ukraine" On Legal Regime "measures related to the formation of military administrations," the document will be available.

The decree provides for the creation:

  • Rural Military Administration in the village of Vinogradovo, Kherson District * City Military Administration in Skadovsk, Kherson region
